	<body>
		<category name="RarityMatchingItemGlowsV3">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Gives the glowy bits on weapons/grenades a change of color to match their rarity. You can have it apply to non-elemental versions only (On by default for everything except Jakobs, applies to weapons only), or all versions.</comment>
				<comment>Note;</comment>
				<comment>Gemstone glows override the elemental glows, there isn't a way around this.</comment>
				<comment>If you're using mods that change the rarity of a weapon or grenade, there are overrides that allow you to change the glow to match the rarity of your modded weapon (Unique, Legendary, Pearlescent, Seraph, or the Uniques from my BL1-Style Rarities).</comment>
				<comment>Examples;</comment>
				<comment>http://imgur.com/a/4TF9w</comment>
			</category>
			<category name="Code">
				<category name="Item Glows">
					<category name="Weapons">
						<category name="No Elemental Glow Override">
							<category name="Whites">
								<category name="Bandit">
									<category name="Pistols">
										<code profiles="default">set GD_Weap_Pistol.Body.Pistol_Body_Bandit MaterialVectorParameterValues ((ParameterName="p_EmissiveColor",ParameterValue=(R=2.550000,G=2.550000,B=2.550000,A=1.000000),ExpressionGUID=(A=1475816242,B=1139906328,C=-187360584,D=-1825963319)))</code>
									</category>
